## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Java Dependency Injection with Kafka Plugin Architecture

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/kafka that implement the plugin/extension loading system: the PluginClassLoader, the plugin scanning via reflection, and the interface-based dependency injection used for Connector, Converter, and HeaderConverter plugins.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

```json
{

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

## Kafka Plugin/Extension Loading System

The system is implemented across **24 main source files** in `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489`:

### Core Isolation Package (`connect/runtime/.../isolation/`)
| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `PluginClassLoader.java` | Extends URLClassLoader; provides isolated class loading per plugin |
| `PluginClassLoaderFactory.java` | Interface for creating PluginClassLoader instances |
| `ClassLoaderFactory.java` | Concrete factory; creates DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader |
| `DelegatingClassLoader.java` | Parent classloader; delegates to PluginClassLoaders (child-first) |
| `LoaderSwap.java` | AutoCloseable; swaps thread context classloader during plugin calls |
| `Plugins.java` | Central facade; orchestrates scanning, registration, and instantiation |
| `PluginScanner.java` | Abstract base for scanning strategies |
| `ReflectionScanner.java` | Scans via ClassGraph reflection library |
| `ServiceLoaderScanner.java` | Scans via Java ServiceLoader (META-INF/services) |
| `PluginScanResult.java` | Container for discovered plugin descriptors |
| `PluginSource.java` | Record for a plugin source location + classloader |
| `PluginDesc.java` | Descriptor: class, version, type, classloader |
| `PluginType.java` | Enum of all plugin types (SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, etc.) |
| `PluginUtils.java` | Utilities for path scanning and version ranges |
| `PluginDiscoveryMode.java` | Enum: ONLY_SCAN, SERVICE_LOAD, HYBRID_WARN, HYBRID_FAIL |
| `PluginsRecommenders.java` | ConfigDef recommenders for plugin config options |
| `VersionedPluginLoadingException.java` | Exception for versioned plugin loading failures |

### Plugin Interfaces (`connect/api/.../`

Each plugin gets its own PluginClassLoader instance, enabling class isolation between plugins.\\n- **PluginClassLoaderFactory.java**: Interface for creating PluginClassLoader instances (used for mocking in tests).\\n- **ClassLoaderFactory.java**: Concrete factory implementing PluginClassLoaderFactory; creates both DelegatingClassLoader and PluginClassLoader instances using SecurityManagerCompatibility.doPrivileged().\\n- **DelegatingClassLoader.java**: The parent classloader that delegates to PluginClassLoaders for isolated plugins or to the system classloader for classpath plugins. Key methods: pluginClassLoader(), installDiscoveredPlugins(), loadVersionedPluginClass().\\n- **LoaderSwap.java**: AutoCloseable utility that swaps the thread context classloader to the plugin's classloader during plugin method invocations, then restores it on close.\\n\\n## 2. Plugin Scanning via Reflection (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/isolation/)\\n\\n- **PluginScanner.java**: Abstract base class for plugin scanning strategies. Defines discoverPlugins(Set<PluginSource>) and abstract scanPlugins(PluginSource).\\n- **ReflectionScanner.java**: Uses the ClassGraph library to scan classpath/plugin JARs via reflection, finding all concrete classes that implement the plugin interfaces (SinkConnector, SourceConnector, Converter, HeaderConverter, Transformation, Predicate, ConfigProvider, ConnectRestExtension, ConnectorClientConfigOverridePolicy).\\n- **ServiceLoaderScanner.java**: Uses Java's ServiceLoader mechanism to discover plugins registered via META-INF/services files.\\n- **PluginScanResult.java**: Container holding sorted sets of PluginDesc for each plugin type discovered during scanning.\\n- **PluginSource.java**: Record representing a plugin source location (classpath or isolated JAR directory) with its associated classloader and URLs.\\n- **PluginDesc.java**: Descriptor for a discovered plugin, holding the class, version, type, and classloader.\\n- **PluginType.java**: Enum of all supported plugin types (SOURCE, SINK, CONVERTER, HEADER_CONVERTER, TRANSFORMATION, PREDICATE, CONFIG_PROVIDER, REST_EXTENSION, CONNECTOR_CLIENT_CONFIG_POLICY).\\n- **PluginUtils.java**: Utilities for building plugin sources from paths, scanning JAR/ZIP/class files, and version range handling.\\n- **PluginDiscoveryMode.java**: Enum controlling how plugins are discovered (ONLY_SCAN, SERVICE_LOAD, HYBRID_WARN, HYBRID_FAIL).\\n\\n## 3.
